There\n/// is no \"pass\" interface in LLVM per se. Instead, an instance of any class\n/// which supports a method to 'run' it over a unit of IR can be used as\n/// a pass. A pass manager is generally a tool to collect a sequence of passes\n/// which run over a particular IR construct, and run each of them in sequence\n/// over each such construct in the containing IR construct. As there is no\n/// containing IR construct for a Module, a manager for passes over modules\n/// forms the base case which runs its managed passes in sequence over the\n/// single module provided.\n///\n/// The core IR library provides managers for running passes over\n/// modules and functions.\n///\n/// * FunctionPassManager can run over a Module, runs each pass over\n///   a Function.\n/// * ModulePassManager must be directly run, runs each pass over the Module.\n///\n/// Note that the implementations of the pass managers use concept-based\n/// polymorphism as outlined in the \"Value Semantics and Concept-based\n/// Polymorphism\" talk (or its abbreviated sibling \"Inheritance Is The Base\n/// Class of Evil\") by Sean Parent:\n/// * https://sean-parent.stlab.cc/papers-and-presentations\n/// * http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=_BpMYeUFXv8\n/// * https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/shows/goingnative-2013/inheritance-base-class-of-evil\n///\n//===----------------------------------------------------------------------===//\n\n#ifndef LLVM_IR_PASSMANAGER_H\n#define LLVM_IR_PASSMANAGER_H\n\n#include \"llvm/ADT/DenseMap.h\"\n#include \"llvm/ADT/STLExtras.h\"\n#include \"llvm/ADT/StringExtras.h\"\n#include \"llvm/ADT/StringRef.h\"\n#include \"llvm/ADT/TinyPtrVector.h\"\n#include \"llvm/IR/Analysis.h\"\n#include \"llvm/IR/PassManagerInternal.h\"\n#include \"llvm/Support/Compiler.h\"\n#include \"llvm/Support/TypeName.h\"\n#include <cassert>\n#include <cstring>\n#include <list>\n#include <memory>\n#include <tuple>\n#include <type_traits>\n#include <utility>\n#include <vector>\n\nnamespace llvm {\n\nclass Function;\nclass Module;\n\n// Forward declare the analysis manager template.\ntemplate <typename IRUnitT, typename... ExtraArgTs> class AnalysisManager;\n\n/// A CRTP mix-in to automatically provide informational APIs needed for\n/// passes.\n///\n/// This provides some boilerplate for types that are passes.\ntemplate <typename DerivedT> struct PassInfoMixin {\n  /// Gets the name of the pass we are mixed into.\n  static StringRef name() {\n    static_assert(std::is_base_of<PassInfoMixin, DerivedT>::value,\n                  \"Must pass the derived type as the template argument!\");\n    StringRef Name = getTypeName<DerivedT>();\n    Name.consume_front(\"llvm::\");\n    return Name;\n  }\n\n  void printPipeline(raw_ostream &OS,\n                     function_ref<StringRef(StringRef)> MapClassName2PassName) {\n    StringRef ClassName = DerivedT::name();\n    auto PassName = MapClassName2PassName(ClassName);\n    OS << PassName;\n  }\n};\n\n/// A CRTP mix-in that provides informational APIs needed for analysis passes.\n///\n/// This provides some boilerplate for types that are analysis passes. It\n/// automatically mixes in \\c PassInfoMixin.\ntemplate <typename DerivedT>\nstruct AnalysisInfoMixin : PassInfoMixin<DerivedT> {\n  /// Returns an opaque, unique ID for this analysis type.\n  ///\n  /// This ID is a pointer type that is guaranteed to be 8-byte aligned and thus\n  /// suitable for use in sets, maps, and other data structures that use the low\n  /// bits of pointers.\n  ///\n  /// Note that this requires the derived type provide a static \\c AnalysisKey\n  /// member called \\c Key.\n  ///\n  /// FIXME: The only reason the mixin type itself can't declare the Key value\n  /// is that some compilers cannot correctly unique a templated static variable\n  /// so it has the same addresses in each instantiation. The only currently\n  /// known platform with this limitation is Windows DLL builds, specifically\n  /// building each part of LLVM as a DLL. If we ever remove that build\n  /// configuration, this mixin can provide the static key as well.\n  static AnalysisKey *ID() {\n    static_assert(std::is_base_of<AnalysisInfoMixin, DerivedT>::value,\n                  \"Must pass the derived type as the template argument!\");\n    return &DerivedT::Key;\n  }\n};\n\nnamespace detail {\n\n/// Actual unpacker of extra arguments in getAnalysisResult,\n/// passes only those tuple arguments that are mentioned in index_sequence.\ntemplate <typename PassT, typename IRUnitT, typename AnalysisManagerT,\n          typename... ArgTs, size_t... Ns>\ntypename PassT::Result\ngetAnalysisResultUnpackTuple(AnalysisManagerT &AM, IRUnitT &IR,\n                             std::tuple<ArgTs...> Args,\n                             std::index_sequence<Ns...>) {\n  (void)Args;\n  return AM.template getResult<PassT>(IR, std::get<Ns>(Args)...);\n}\n\n/// Helper for *partial* unpacking of extra arguments in getAnalysisResult.\n///\n/// Arguments passed in tuple come from PassManager, so they might have extra\n/// arguments after those AnalysisManager's ExtraArgTs ones that we need to\n/// pass to getResult.\ntemplate <typename PassT, typename IRUnitT, typename... AnalysisArgTs,\n          typename... MainArgTs>\ntypename PassT::Result\ngetAnalysisResult(AnalysisManager<IRUnitT, AnalysisArgTs...> &AM, IRUnitT &IR,\n                  std::tuple<MainArgTs...> Args) {\n  return (getAnalysisResultUnpackTuple<\n          PassT, IRUnitT>)(AM, IR, Args,\n                           std::index_sequence_for<AnalysisArgTs...>{});\n}\n\n} // namespace detail\n\n/// Manages a sequence of passes over a particular unit of IR.\n///\n/// A pass manager contains a sequence of passes to run over a particular unit\n/// of IR (e.g. Functions, Modules). Eventually they will be suppressed during\n  // codegen, but eliminating here enables more opportunity for GlobalDCE as it\n  // may make globals referenced by available external functions dead and saves\n  // running remaining passes on the eliminated functions. We should at this point have a reasonably minimal\n  // and richly annotated call graph. By computing aliasing and mod/ref\n  // information for all local globals here, the late loop passes and notably\n  // the vectorizer will be able to use them to help recognize vectorizable\n  // memory operations.\n  if (EnableGlobalAnalyses)\n    MPM.addPass(RecomputeGlobalsAAPass());\n\n  invokeOptimizerEarlyEPCallbacks(MPM, Level, LTOPhase);\n\n  FunctionPassManager OptimizePM;\n\n  // Only drop unnecessary assumes post-inline and post-link, as otherwise\n  // additional uses of the affected value may be introduced through inlining\n  // and CSE.\n  if (!isLTOPreLink(LTOPhase))\n    OptimizePM.addPass(DropUnnecessaryAssumesPass());\n\n  // Scheduling LoopVersioningLICM when inlining is over, because after that\n  // we may see more accurate aliasing. Reason to run this late is that too\n  // early versioning may prevent further inlining due to increase of code\n  // size. Other optimizations which runs later might get benefit of no-alias\n  // assumption in clone loop.\n  if (UseLoopVersioningLICM) {\n    OptimizePM.addPass(\n        createFunctionToLoopPassAdaptor(LoopVersioningLICMPass()));\n    // LoopVersioningLICM pass might increase new LICM opportunities.\n    OptimizePM.addPass(createFunctionToLoopPassAdaptor(\n        LICMPass(PTO.LicmMssaOptCap, PTO.LicmMssaNoAccForPromotionCap,\n                 /*AllowSpeculation=*/true),\n        /*USeMemorySSA=*/true));\n  }\n\n  OptimizePM.addPass(Float2IntPass());\n  OptimizePM.addPass(LowerConstantIntrinsicsPass());\n\n  if (EnableMatrix) {\n    OptimizePM.addPass(LowerMatrixIntrinsicsPass());\n    OptimizePM.addPass(EarlyCSEPass());\n  }\n\n  // CHR pass should only be applied with the profile information.\n  // The check is to check the profile summary information in CHR.\n  if (EnableCHR && Level == OptimizationLevel::O3)\n    OptimizePM.addPass(ControlHeightReductionPass());\n\n  // FIXME: We need to run some loop optimizations to re-rotate loops after\n  // simplifycfg and others undo their rotation.\n\n  // Optimize the loop execution. These passes operate on entire loop nests\n  // rather than on each loop in an inside-out manner, and so they are actually\n  // function passes.\n\n  invokeVectorizerStartEPCallbacks(OptimizePM, Level);\n\n  LoopPassManager LPM;\n  // First rotate loops that may have been un-rotated by prior passes.\n  // Disable header duplication at -Oz.\n  LPM.addPass(LoopRotatePass(EnableLoopHeaderDuplication ||\n                                 Level != OptimizationLevel::Oz,\n                             LTOPreLink));\n  // Some loops may have become dead by now. Try to delete them.\n  // FIXME: see discussion in https://reviews.llvm.org/D112851,\n  //        this may need to be revisited once we run GVN before loop deletion\n  //        in the simplification pipeline.\n  LPM.addPass(LoopDeletionPass());\n\n  if (PTO.LoopInterchange)\n    LPM.addPass(LoopInterchangePass());\n\n  OptimizePM.addPass(\n      createFunctionToLoopPassAdaptor(std::move(LPM), /*UseMemorySSA=*/false));\n\n  // FIXME: This may not be the right place in the pipeline.\n  // We need to have the data to support the right place.\n  if (PTO.LoopFusion)\n    OptimizePM.addPass(LoopFusePass());\n\n  // Distribute loops to allow partial vectorization.  I.e. isolate dependences\n  // into separate loop that would otherwise inhibit vectorization.  This is\n  // currently only performed for loops marked with the metadata\n  // llvm.loop.distribute=true or when -enable-loop-distribute is specified.\n  OptimizePM.addPass(LoopDistributePass());\n\n  // Populates the VFABI attribute with the scalar-to-vector mappings\n  // from the TargetLibraryInfo.\n  OptimizePM.addPass(InjectTLIMappings());\n\n  addVectorPasses(Level, OptimizePM, LTOPhase);\n\n  invokeVectorizerEndEPCallbacks(OptimizePM, Level);\n\n  // LoopSink pass sinks instructions hoisted by LICM, which serves as a\n  // canonicalization pass that enables other optimizations. As a result,\n  // LoopSink pass needs to be a very late IR pass to avoid undoing LICM\n  // result too early.\n  OptimizePM.addPass(LoopSinkPass());\n\n  // And finally clean up LCSSA form before generating code.\n  OptimizePM.addPass(InstSimplifyPass());\n\n  // This hoists/decomposes div/rem ops. It should run after other sink/hoist\n  // passes to avoid re-sinking, but before SimplifyCFG because it can allow\n  // flattening of blocks.\n  OptimizePM.addPass(DivRemPairsPass());\n\n  // Try to annotate calls that were created during optimization.\n  OptimizePM.addPass(\n      TailCallElimPass(/*UpdateFunctionEntryCount=*/isInstrumentedPGOUse()));\n\n  // LoopSink (and other loop passes since the last simplifyCFG) might have\n  // resulted in single-entry-single-exit or empty blocks. Clean up the CFG.\n  OptimizePM.addPass(\n      SimplifyCFGPass(SimplifyCFGOptions()\n                          .convertSwitchRangeToICmp(true)\n                          .convertSwitchToArithmetic(true)\n                          .speculateUnpredictables(true)\n                          .hoistLoadsStoresWithCondFaulting(true)));\n\n  // Add the core optimizing pipeline.\n  MPM.addPass(createModuleToFunctionPassAdaptor(std::move(OptimizePM),\n                                                PTO.EagerlyInvalidateAnalyses));\n\n  // AllocToken transforms heap allocation calls; this needs to run late after\n  // other allocation call transformations (such as those in InstCombine).\n  if (!LTOPreLink)\n    MPM.addPass(AllocTokenPass());\n\n  invokeOptimizerLastEPCallbacks(MPM, Level, LTOPhase);\n\n  // Split out cold code. Splitting is done late to avoid hiding context from\n  // other optimizations and inadvertently regressing performance. The tradeoff\n  // is that this has a higher code size cost than splitting early.\n  if (EnableHotColdSplit && !LTOPreLink)\n    MPM.addPass(HotColdSplittingPass());\n\n  // Search the code for similar regions of code. If enough similar regions can\n  // be found where extracting the regions into their own function will decrease\n  // the size of the program, we extract the regions, a deduplicate the\n  // structurally similar regions.\n  if (EnableIROutliner)\n    MPM.addPass(IROutlinerPass());\n\n  // Now we need to do some global optimization transforms.\n  // FIXME: It would seem like these should come first in the optimization\n  // pipeline and maybe be the bottom of the canonicalization pipeline? Weird\n  // ordering here.\n  MPM.addPass(GlobalDCEPass());\n  MPM.addPass(ConstantMergePass());\n\n  // Merge functions if requested. It has a better chance to merge functions\n  // after ConstantMerge folded jump tables.\n  if (PTO.MergeFunctions)\n    MPM.addPass(MergeFunctionsPass());\n\n  if (PTO.CallGraphProfile && !LTOPreLink)\n    MPM.addPass(CGProfilePass(isLTOPostLink(LTOPhase)));\n\n  // RelLookupTableConverterPass runs later in LTO post-link pipeline.\n  if (!LTOPreLink)\n    MPM.addPass(RelLookupTableConverterPass());\n\n  // Add devirtualization pass only when LTO is not enabled, as otherwise\n  // the pass is already enabled in the LTO pipeline.\n  if (PTO.DevirtualizeSpeculatively && LTOPhase == ThinOrFullLTOPhase::None) {\n    // TODO: explore a better pipeline configuration that can improve\n    // compilation time overhead.\n    MPM.addPass(WholeProgramDevirtPass(\n        /*ExportSummary*/ nullptr,\n        /*ImportSummary*/ nullptr,\n        /*DevirtSpeculatively*/ PTO.DevirtualizeSpeculatively));\n    MPM.addPass(LowerTypeTestsPass(nullptr, nullptr,\n                                   lowertypetests::DropTestKind::Assume));\n    // Given that the devirtualization creates more opportunities for inlining,\n    // we run the Inliner again here to maximize the optimization gain we\n    // get from devirtualization.\n    // Also, we can't run devirtualization before inlining because the\n    // devirtualization depends on the passes optimizing/eliminating vtable GVs\n    // and those passes are only effective after inlining.\n    if (EnableModuleInliner) {\n      MPM.addPass(ModuleInlinerPass(getInlineParamsFromOptLevel(Level),\n                                    UseInlineAdvisor,\n                                    ThinOrFullLTOPhase::None));\n    } else {\n      MPM.addPass(ModuleInlinerWrapperPass(\n          getInlineParamsFromOptLevel(Level),\n          /* MandatoryFirst */ true,\n          InlineContext{ThinOrFullLTOPhase::None, InlinePass::CGSCCInliner}));\n    }\n  }\n  return MPM;\n}\n\nModulePassManager\nPassBuilder::buildPerModuleDefaultPipeline(OptimizationLevel Level,\n                                           ThinOrFullLTOPhase Phase) {\n  if (Level == OptimizationLevel::O0)\n    return buildO0DefaultPipeline(Level, Phase);\n\n  ModulePassManager MPM;\n\n  // Currently this pipeline is only invoked in an LTO pre link pass or when we\n  // are not running LTO. If that changes the below checks may need updating.\n  assert(isLTOPreLink(Phase) || Phase == ThinOrFullLTOPhase::None);\n\n  // If we are invoking this in non-LTO mode, remove any MemProf related","numLines":250,"startLine":1478,"totalLines":2485}}}

These classes should be explicitly instantiated for any IR unit,\n    11→/// and files doing the explicit instantiation should include this header.\n    12→///\n    13→//===----------------------------------------------------------------------===//\n    14→\n    15→#ifndef LLVM_IR_PASSMANAGERIMPL_H\n    16→#define LLVM_IR_PASSMANAGERIMPL_H\n    17→\n    18→#include \"llvm/IR/Function.h\"\n    19→#include \"llvm/IR/PassInstrumentation.h\"\n    20→#include \"llvm/IR/PassManager.h\"\n    21→#include \"llvm/Support/CommandLine.h\"\n    22→#include \"llvm/Support/Compiler.h\"\n    23→#include \"llvm/Support/PrettyStackTrace.h\"\n    24→\n    25→namespace llvm {\n    26→\n    27→template <typename IRUnitT, typename AnalysisManagerT, typename... ExtraArgTs>\n    28→PreservedAnalyses PassManager<IRUnitT, AnalysisManagerT, ExtraArgTs...>::run(\n    29→    IRUnitT &IR, AnalysisManagerT &AM, ExtraArgTs... ExtraArgs) {\n    30→  class StackTraceEntry : public PrettyStackTraceEntry {\n    31→    const PassInstrumentation &PI;\n    32→    IRUnitT &IR;\n    33→    PassConceptT *Pass = nullptr;\n    34→\n    35→  public:\n    36→    explicit StackTraceEntry(const PassInstrumentation &PI, IRUnitT &IR)\n    37→        : PI(PI), IR(IR) {}\n    38→\n    39→    void setPass(PassConceptT *P) { Pass = P; }\n    40→\n    41→    void print(raw_ostream &OS) const override {\n    42→      OS << \"Running pass \\\"\";\n    43→      if (Pass)\n    44→        Pass->printPipeline(OS, [this](StringRef ClassName) {\n    45→          auto PassName = PI.getPassNameForClassName(ClassName);\n    46→          return PassName.empty() ? ClassName : PassName;\n    47→        });\n    48→      else\n    49→        OS << \"unknown\";\n    50→      OS << \"\\\" on \";\n    51→      printIRUnitNameForStackTrace(OS, IR);\n    52→      OS << \"\\n\";\n    53→    }\n    54→  };\n    55→\n    56→  PreservedAnalyses PA = PreservedAnalyses::all();\n    57→\n    58→  // Request PassInstrumentation from analysis manager, will use it to run\n    59→  // instrumenting callbacks for the passes later.\n    60→  // Here we use std::tuple wrapper over getResult which helps to extract\n    61→  // AnalysisManager's arguments out of the whole ExtraArgs set.\n    62→  PassInstrumentation PI =\n    63→      detail::getAnalysisResult<PassInstrumentationAnalysis>(\n    64→          AM, IR, std::tuple<ExtraArgTs...>(ExtraArgs...));\n    65→\n    66→  StackTraceEntry Entry(PI, IR);\n    67→  for (auto &Pass : Passes) {\n    68→    Entry.setPass(&*Pass);\n    69→\n    70→    // Check the PassInstrumentation's BeforePass callbacks before running the\n    71→    // pass, skip its execution completely if asked to (callback returns\n    72→    // false).\n    73→    if (!PI.runBeforePass<IRUnitT>(*Pass, IR))\n    74→      continue;\n    75→\n    76→    PreservedAnalyses PassPA = Pass->run(IR, AM, ExtraArgs...);\n    77→\n    78→    // Update the analysis manager as each pass runs and potentially\n    79→    // invalidates analyses.\n    80→    AM.invalidate(IR, PassPA);\n    81→\n    82→    // Call onto PassInstrumentation's AfterPass callbacks immediately after\n    83→    // running the pass.\n    84→    PI.runAfterPass<IRUnitT>(*Pass, IR, PassPA);\n    85→\n    86→    // Finally, intersect the preserved analyses to compute the aggregate\n    87→    // preserved set for this pass manager.\n    88→    PA.intersect(std::move(PassPA));\n    89→  }\n    90→\n    91→  // Invalidation was handled after each pass in the above loop for the\n    92→  // current unit of IR. Therefore, the remaining analysis results in the\n    93→  // AnalysisManager are preserved. We mark this with a set so that we don't\n    94→  // need to inspect each one individually.\n    95→  PA.preserveSet<AllAnalysesOn<IRUnitT>>();\n    96→\n    97→  return PA;\n    98→}\n    99→\n   100→template <typename IRUnitT, typename... ExtraArgTs>\n   101→inline AnalysisManager<IRUnitT, ExtraArgTs...>::AnalysisManager() = default;\n   102→\n   103→template <typename IRUnitT, typename... ExtraArgTs>\n   104→inline AnalysisManager<IRUnitT, ExtraArgTs...>::AnalysisManager(\n   105→    AnalysisManager &&) = default;\n   106→\n   107→template <typename IRUnitT, typename... ExtraArgTs>\n   108→inline AnalysisManager<IRUnitT, ExtraArgTs...> &\n   109→AnalysisManager<IRUnitT, ExtraArgTs...>::operator=(AnalysisManager &&) =\n   110→    default;\n   111→\n   112→template <typename IRUnitT, typename... ExtraArgTs>\n   113→inline void\n   114→AnalysisManager<IRUnitT, ExtraArgTs...>::clear(IRUnitT &IR,\n   115→                                               llvm::StringRef Name) {\n   116→  if (auto *PI = getCachedResult<PassInstrumentationAnalysis>(IR))\n   117→    PI->runAnalysesCleared(Name);\n   118→\n   119→  auto ResultsListI = AnalysisResultLists.find(&IR);\n   120→  if (ResultsListI == AnalysisResultLists.end())\n   121→    return;\n   122→  // Delete the map entries that point into the results list.\n   123→  for (auto &IDAndResult : ResultsListI->second)\n   124→    AnalysisResults.erase({IDAndResult.first, &IR});\n   125→\n   126→  // And actually destroy and erase the results associated with this IR.\n   127→  AnalysisResultLists.erase(ResultsListI);\n   128→}\n   129→\n   130→template <typename IRUnitT, typename... ExtraArgTs>\n   131→inline typename AnalysisManager<IRUnitT, ExtraArgTs...>::ResultConceptT &\n   132→AnalysisManager<IRUnitT, ExtraArgTs...>::getResultImpl(\n   133→    AnalysisKey *ID, IRUnitT &IR, ExtraArgTs... ExtraArgs) {\n   134→  auto [RI, Inserted] = AnalysisResults.try_emplace(std::make_pair(ID, &IR));\n   135→\n   136→  // If we don't have a cached result for this function, look up the pass and\n   137→  // run it to produce a result, which we then add to the cache.\n   138→  if (Inserted) {\n   139→    auto &P = this->lookUpPass(ID);\n   140→\n   141→    PassInstrumentation PI;\n   142→    if (ID != PassInstrumentationAnalysis::ID()) {\n   143→      PI = getResult<PassInstrumentationAnalysis>(IR, ExtraArgs...);\n   144→      PI.runBeforeAnalysis(P, IR);\n   145→    }\n   146→\n   147→    AnalysisResultListT &ResultList = AnalysisResultLists[&IR];\n   148→    ResultList.emplace_back(ID, P.run(IR, *this, ExtraArgs...));\n   149→\n   150→    PI.runAfterAnalysis(P, IR);\n   151→\n   152→    // P.run may have inserted elements into AnalysisResults and invalidated\n   153→    // RI.\n   154→    RI = AnalysisResults.find({ID, &IR});\n   155→    assert(RI != AnalysisResults.end() && \"we just inserted it!\");\n   156→\n   157→    RI->second = std::prev(ResultList.end());\n   158→  }\n   159→\n   160→  return *RI->second->second;\n   161→}\n   162→\n   163→template <typename IRUnitT, typename... ExtraArgTs>\n   164→inline void AnalysisManager<IRUnitT, ExtraArgTs...>::invalidate(\n   165→    IRUnitT &IR, const PreservedAnalyses &PA) {\n   166→  // We're done if all analyses on this IR unit are preserved.\n   167→  if (PA.allAnalysesInSetPreserved<AllAnalysesOn<IRUnitT>>())\n   168→    return;\n   169→\n   170→  // Track whether each analysis's result is invalidated in\n   171→  // IsResultInvalidated.\n   172→  SmallDenseMap<AnalysisKey *, bool, 8> IsResultInvalidated;\n   173→  Invalidator Inv(IsResultInvalidated, AnalysisResults);\n   174→  AnalysisResultListT &ResultsList = AnalysisResultLists[&IR];\n   175→  for (auto &AnalysisResultPair : ResultsList) {\n   176→    // This is basically the same thing as Invalidator::invalidate, but we\n   177→    // can't call it here because we're operating on the type-erased result.\n   178→    // Moreover if we instead called invalidate() directly, it would do an\n   179→    // unnecessary look up in ResultsList.\n   180→ These classes should be explicitly instantiated for any IR unit,\n/// and files doing the explicit instantiation should include this header.\n///\n//===----------------------------------------------------------------------===//\n\n#ifndef LLVM_IR_PASSMANAGERIMPL_H\n#define LLVM_IR_PASSMANAGERIMPL_H\n\n#include \"llvm/IR/Function.h\"\n#include \"llvm/IR/PassInstrumentation.h\"\n#include \"llvm/IR/PassManager.h\"\n#include \"llvm/Support/CommandLine.h\"\n#include \"llvm/Support/Compiler.h\"\n#include \"llvm/Support/PrettyStackTrace.h\"\n\nnamespace llvm {\n\ntemplate <typename IRUnitT, typename AnalysisManagerT, typename... ExtraArgTs>\nPreservedAnalyses PassManager<IRUnitT, AnalysisManagerT, ExtraArgTs...>::run(\n    IRUnitT &IR, AnalysisManagerT &AM, ExtraArgTs... ExtraArgs) {\n  class StackTraceEntry : public PrettyStackTraceEntry {\n    const PassInstrumentation &PI;\n    IRUnitT &IR;\n    PassConceptT *Pass = nullptr;\n\n  public:\n    explicit StackTraceEntry(const PassInstrumentation &PI, IRUnitT &IR)\n        : PI(PI), IR(IR) {}\n\n    void setPass(PassConceptT *P) { Pass = P; }\n\n    void print(raw_ostream &OS) const override {\n      OS << \"Running pass \\\"\";\n      if (Pass)\n        Pass->printPipeline(OS, [this](StringRef ClassName) {\n          auto PassName = PI.getPassNameForClassName(ClassName);\n          return PassName.empty() ? ClassName : PassName;\n        });\n      else\n        OS << \"unknown\";\n      OS << \"\\\" on \";\n      printIRUnitNameForStackTrace(OS, IR);\n      OS << \"\\n\";\n    }\n  };\n\n  PreservedAnalyses PA = PreservedAnalyses::all();\n\n  // Request PassInstrumentation from analysis manager, will use it to run\n  // instrumenting callbacks for the passes later.\n  // Here we use std::tuple wrapper over getResult which helps to extract\n  // AnalysisManager's arguments out of the whole ExtraArgs set.\n  PassInstrumentation PI =\n      detail::getAnalysisResult<PassInstrumentationAnalysis>(\n          AM, IR, std::tuple<ExtraArgTs...>(ExtraArgs...));\n\n  StackTraceEntry Entry(PI, IR);\n  for (auto &Pass : Passes) {\n    Entry.setPass(&*Pass);\n\n    // Check the PassInstrumentation's BeforePass callbacks before running the\n    // pass, skip its execution completely if asked to (callback returns\n    // false).\n    if (!PI.runBeforePass<IRUnitT>(*Pass, IR))\n      continue;\n\n    PreservedAnalyses PassPA = Pass->run(IR, AM, ExtraArgs...);\n\n    // Update the analysis manager as each pass runs and potentially\n    // invalidates analyses.\n    AM.invalidate(IR, PassPA);\n\n    // Call onto PassInstrumentation's AfterPass callbacks immediately after\n    // running the pass.\n    PI.runAfterPass<IRUnitT>(*Pass, IR, PassPA);\n\n    // Finally, intersect the preserved analyses to compute the aggregate\n    // preserved set for this pass manager.\n    PA.intersect(std::move(PassPA));\n  }\n\n  // Invalidation was handled after each pass in the above loop for the\n  // current unit of IR. Therefore, the remaining analysis results in the\n  // AnalysisManager are preserved. We mark this with a set so that we don't\n  // need to inspect each one individually.\n  PA.preserveSet<AllAnalysesOn<IRUnitT>>();\n\n  return PA;\n}\n\ntemplate <typename IRUnitT, typename... ExtraArgTs>\ninline AnalysisManager<IRUnitT, ExtraArgTs...>::AnalysisManager() = default;\n\ntemplate <typename IRUnitT, typename... ExtraArgTs>\ninline AnalysisManager<IRUnitT, ExtraArgTs...>::AnalysisManager(\n    AnalysisManager &&) = default;\n\ntemplate <typename IRUnitT, typename... ExtraArgTs>\ninline AnalysisManager<IRUnitT, ExtraArgTs...> &\nAnalysisManager<IRUnitT, ExtraArgTs...>::operator=(AnalysisManager &&) =\n    default;\n\ntemplate <typename IRUnitT, typename... ExtraArgTs>\ninline void\nAnalysisManager<IRUnitT, ExtraArgTs...>::clear(IRUnitT &IR,\n                                               llvm::StringRef Name) {\n  if (auto *PI = getCachedResult<PassInstrumentationAnalysis>(IR))\n    PI->runAnalysesCleared(Name);\n\n  auto ResultsListI = AnalysisResultLists.find(&IR);\n  if (ResultsListI == AnalysisResultLists.end())\n    return;\n  // Delete the map entries that point into the results list.\n  for (auto &IDAndResult : ResultsListI->second)\n    AnalysisResults.erase({IDAndResult.first, &IR});\n\n  // And actually destroy and erase the results associated with this IR.\n  AnalysisResultLists.erase(ResultsListI);\n}\n\ntemplate <typename IRUnitT, typename... ExtraArgTs>\ninline typename AnalysisManager<IRUnitT, ExtraArgTs...>::ResultConceptT &\nAnalysisManager<IRUnitT, ExtraArgTs...>::getResultImpl(\n    AnalysisKey *ID, IRUnitT &IR, ExtraArgTs... ExtraArgs) {\n  auto [RI, Inserted] = AnalysisResults.try_emplace(std::make_pair(ID, &IR));\n\n  // If we don't have a cached result for this function, look up the pass and\n  // run it to produce a result, which we then add to the cache.\n  if (Inserted) {\n    auto &P = this->lookUpPass(ID);\n\n    PassInstrumentation PI;\n    if (ID != PassInstrumentationAnalysis::ID()) {\n      PI = getResult<PassInstrumentationAnalysis>(IR, ExtraArgs...);\n      PI.runBeforeAnalysis(P, IR);\n    }\n\n    AnalysisResultListT &ResultList = AnalysisResultLists[&IR];\n    ResultList.emplace_back(ID, P.run(IR, *this, ExtraArgs...));\n\n    PI.runAfterAnalysis(P, IR);\n\n    // P.run may have inserted elements into AnalysisResults and invalidated\n    // RI.\n    RI = AnalysisResults.find({ID, &IR});\n    assert(RI != AnalysisResults.end() && \"we just inserted it!\");\n\n    RI->second = std::prev(ResultList.end());\n  }\n\n  return *RI->second->second;\n}\n\ntemplate <typename IRUnitT, typename... ExtraArgTs>\ninline void AnalysisManager<IRUnitT, ExtraArgTs...>::invalidate(\n    IRUnitT &IR, const PreservedAnalyses &PA) {\n  // We're done if all analyses on this IR unit are preserved.\n  if (PA.allAnalysesInSetPreserved<AllAnalysesOn<IRUnitT>>())\n    return;\n\n  // Track whether each analysis's result is invalidated in\n  // IsResultInvalidated.\n  SmallDenseMap<AnalysisKey *, bool, 8> IsResultInvalidated;\n  Invalidator Inv(IsResultInvalidated, AnalysisResults);\n  AnalysisResultListT &ResultsList = AnalysisResultLists[&IR];\n  for (auto &AnalysisResultPair : ResultsList) {\n    // This is basically the same thing as Invalidator::invalidate, but we\n    // can't call it here because we're operating on the type-erased result.\n    // Moreover if we instead called invalidate() directly, it would do an\n    // unnecessary look up in ResultsList.\n    AnalysisKey *ID = AnalysisResultPair.first;\n    auto &Result = *AnalysisResultPair.second;\n\n    auto IMapI = IsResultInvalidated.find(ID);\n    if (IMapI != IsResultInvalidated.end())\n      // This result was already handled via the Invalidator.\n      continue;\n\n    // Try to invalidate the result, giving it the Invalidator so it can\n    // recursively query for any dependencies it has and record the result.\n    // Note that we cannot reuse 'IMapI' here or pre-insert the ID, as\n    // Result.invalidate may insert things into the map, invalidating our\n    // iterator.\n    bool Inserted =\n        IsResultInvalidated.insert({ID, Result.invalidate(IR, PA, Inv)}).second;\n    (void)Inserted;\n    assert(Inserted && \"Should never have already inserted this ID, likely \"\n                       \"indicates a cycle!\");\n  }\n\n  // Now erase the results that were marked above as invalidated.","numLines":200,"startLine":1,"totalLines":223}}}

ExtraArgTs>\nstruct PassConcept {\n  // Boiler plate necessary for the container of derived classes.\n  virtual ~PassConcept() = default;\n\n  /// The polymorphic API which runs the pass over a given IR entity.\n  ///\n  /// Note that actual pass object can omit the analysis manager argument if\n  /// desired. A pass class derives from PassInfoMixin<PassName> (e.g., InstCombinePass)\n2. Passes are registered in PassRegistry.def with macro definitions\n3. The PassManager template manages a vector of PassConcept pointers\n4. When a pass is added via addPass(), it's wrapped in a PassModel which derives from PassConcept\n\n\n5. It implements addPass<PassT>() which wraps each pass in a PassModel<IRUnitT, PassT> that derives from PassConcept. PassModel is a template that wraps any pass class and implements the concept, calling the pass's run() method. **PassConcept & PassModel** (`llvm/include/llvm/IR/PassManagerInternal.h`): Type-erased polymorphic pattern where PassModel wraps any pass class implementing the PassConcept interface\n\n3. **PassInfoMixin** (`llvm/include/llvm/IR/PassManager.h`): CRTP mixin providing pass naming and pipeline printing\n\n4. **PassRegistry** (`llvm/include/llvm/PassRegistry.h`): Manages global pass registration and lookup\n\n### **Registration & Parsing:**\n\n- **PassRegistry.def** (`llvm/lib/Passes/PassRegistry.def`): Macro-based registry mapping string names to pass constructors\n- **PassBuilder** (`llvm/lib/Passes/PassBuilder.cpp`): Parses pass pipeline strings and instantiates passes\n\n### **O2/O3 Optimization Pipeline:**\n\nThe optimization pipeline hierarchy in `PassBuilderPipelines.cpp`:\n- `buildPerModuleDefaultPipeline()` → Main entry point\n- `buildModuleSimplificationPipeline()` → Early canonicalization passes\n- `buildModuleOptimizationPipeline()` → Main optimizations (with O3-specific passes like ControlHeightReduction)\n\n**Output file created:** `/workspace/answer.json` containing complete file references, key symbols, and the execution
